  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_334d3b06-c94f-4b22-b9f3-8fb87981b99f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText16668557526963075575" style="display:none">Charlie, a highly-strung, openly gay over-thinker, and Nick, a cheerful, soft-hearted rugby player, meet at a British all-boys grammar school. Friendship blooms quickly, but could there be something more...?<br /><br />Charlie Spring is in Year 10 at Truham Grammar School for Boys. The past year hasn't been too great, but at least he's not being bullied anymore. Nick Nelson is in Year 11 and on the school rugby team. He's heard a little about Charlie - the kid who was outed last year and bullied for a few months - but he's never had the opportunity to talk to him.<br />They quickly become friends, and soon Charlie is falling hard for Nick, even though he doesn't think he has a chance. But love works in surprising ways, and sometimes good things are waiting just around the corner...</span>
  <a data-text-id="16668557526963075575" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

        if (this.up('#box')) {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_42192440').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_42192440').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_42192440').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });
      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_sort_order_span_tip_687').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>
</div>

<div id="review_3105548588" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3105548588" />
    <a title="Larry H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5872506-larry-h"><img alt="Larry H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577826084p2/5872506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3105548588?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Larry H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Larry H" href="/user/show/5872506-larry-h">Larry H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3105548588" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14364319041771247372">Alice Oseman's <b>
  <i>Heartstopper</i>
</b> is a beautifully poignant graphic novel about identity, friendship, crushes, and the flush of first love.<br/><br/>Most people in school seem to know that Charlie is gay. He’s taken some bullying for it, and it’s toyed with his self-esteem and what he thinks he deserves in terms of relationships, but for the most part, life isn’t too bad.<br/><br/>One day Charlie gets assigned to a new classroom and sits next to Nick Nelson, who is a grade ahead of him. Nick is tall, muscular, popula</span>
  <span id="freeText14364319041771247372" style="display:none">Alice Oseman's <b>
  <i>Heartstopper</i>
</b> is a beautifully poignant graphic novel about identity, friendship, crushes, and the flush of first love.<br /><br />Most people in school seem to know that Charlie is gay. He’s taken some bullying for it, and it’s toyed with his self-esteem and what he thinks he deserves in terms of relationships, but for the most part, life isn’t too bad.<br /><br />One day Charlie gets assigned to a new classroom and sits next to Nick Nelson, who is a grade ahead of him. Nick is tall, muscular, popular, a real “rugby lad.” But while Charlie expects Nick to ignore him, the two quickly strike up a real friendship.<br /><br />As their friendship grows (Nick even gets Charlie to play rugby), and Nick even rescues Charlie from a potentially messy situation, Charlie can’t believe that he’s crushing on a straight guy. But why is it that Nick can’t stop thinking about Charlie, too?<br /><br />Ah, this was amazing. It was so endearing, so wonderfully drawn, that I fell in love with this almost immediately. I read it quickly and was sad that it was over—I immediately ordered volume 2, which should arrive Sunday!! (Volume 3 is due out in February.)<br /><br />The title of this book isn’t quite accurate. I’d call it <b>
  <i>Heartgrabber</i>
</b>, because it took hold of my heart and won’t let go. I've really been loving graphic novels lately and feel like these stories really lend themselves to being told in this format. And as much as I love conjuring up images of what I read in my own head, sometimes it's great to see what the author or illustrator had in mind.<br /><br />Once again, I’m so happy that books like this exist today, to let LGBTQIA+ kids—and adults—see that who they choose to love doesn’t doom them to loneliness. No one's road is perfectly easy, but it's nice to have books like this as companions along the journey.<br /><br />See all of my reviews at <a href="http://itseithersadnessoreuphoria.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">itseithersadnessoreuphoria.blogspot.com</a>.<br /><br />You can follow me on Instagram at <a href="https://www.instagram.com/the.bookishworld.of.yrralh/" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener"> https://www.instagram.com/the.bookishworld.of.yrralh/.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14364319041771247372" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17658953846571681539">How adorable! <br/><br/>3.5 ⭐️<br/><br/>This was my first graphic novel and it was so damn cute!<br/><br/>Charlie and Nick are one school year apart, they've never spoken before until they are seated next to each other in their tutor group. <br/>Soon their acquaintance evolves into friendship.   <span id="freeText17658953846571681539" style="display:none">How adorable! <br /><br />3.5 ⭐️<br /><br />This was my first graphic novel and it was so damn cute!<br /><br />Charlie and Nick are one school year apart, they've never spoken before until they are seated next to each other in their tutor group. <br />Soon their acquaintance evolves into friendship. Charlie joins the school rugby team that Nick is on and they realise they have more in common than they first thought. <br /><br />There is so much more to this book than meets the eye. Characters discovering their sexuality, dealing with bullying and homophobia, there is even a scene dealing with consent and sexual harassment. <br /><br />I can't wait to see how Nick and Charlie's relationship continues! </span>

I’m going to disappear now, and hope that you’ll take the time to make yourself smile, because <i>Heartstopper</i> will give you that for sure.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1582874056908956329">This was the most pure and wholesome thing I have ever read and my heart can't cope with how much I loved it! Nick and Charlie are my new favourite soft boys and deserve all the love and happiness in the world. The rave reviews for this had me almost hesitant to pick it up, so heavy was the adoration it received, but I need not have feared as it was heart-aching perfection!</span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2433501424" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2433501424" />
    <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments"><img alt="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554228831p2/67920559.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2433501424?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments">Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=childhood-lovers">childhood-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=it-hurts">it-hurts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=young-love">young-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=never-forget">never-forget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=tears-are-everywhere">tears-are-everywhere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=sexual-tension">sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2433501424" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4502148319233587612"><i>
  <b>"Yes, I will listen to the rain. I will listen to the mountain bird. Oh, a heartstopper is the solitaire's one note - high, sweet, lonely, magic." </b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736726._SY540_.png' width='700' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736727._SY540_.png' width='700' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b><br/>Here's why it's called <i>Heartstopper</i>.<br/>Somewhere in the middle of those words, and the beautiful art. This story manages to do the following to that 'hollow muscular organ that pumps the blood through the circulatory system': <br/><br/>- Make's it skip. <br/>- Fills it up. <br/>- Stops it dead. <br/>- Starts it up again. <br/><br/>By the time you've experienced Nick and Charlie, you'l</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4502148319233587612" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"Yes, I will listen to the rain. I will listen to the mountain bird. Oh, a heartstopper is the solitaire's one note - high, sweet, lonely, magic." </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736726._SY540_.png" width="700" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736727._SY540_.png" width="700" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><br>Here's why it's called <i>Heartstopper</i>.<br>Somewhere in the middle of those words, and the beautiful art. This story manages to do the following to that 'hollow muscular organ that pumps the blood through the circulatory system': <br><br>- Make's it skip. <br>- Fills it up. <br>- Stops it dead. <br>- Starts it up again. <br><br>By the time you've experienced Nick and Charlie, you'll have your heart in your hands and a smile on your face as you look at it, because it now belongs to both those nerds. </b><br>______________<br><br><u>
  <b>A Note To Me</b>
</u> <br>This is my first ever 5 stars to a graphic novel / comic. I am very very stingy with that last star, and those who know me and my reviews will be able to tell you just what a bitch I am when handing out 4/5 stars. <br><br>It deserved every. single. one. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736728._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In another one of my sequential art reviews I wrote the following: <br><b>Let me tell you a little something about graphic novels. </b><br>The ratio is about 2 part words, and 5 part images. <br>2:5.<br>Ladies and gentlemen. That's not a lot of legroom for authors to work with. <br>They have, what my old design teacher would call - "a very minimal amount of available resources to create a functioning system." <br><br><b>2:5.</b><br><br><i>And some authors can create magic.</i> <br><br>Magic in their shortage of words, picking each and every one out, so that the system not only works but thrives...<br>So that the message goes across in that little word count, and the letters infiltrate pathos in your head. Then, add that to the beautiful artwork that graphic novelists aid their words with - you're left with a substance to your magic. It's the fuel that drives the story to where it's going. <br><br><b>The system needs the fuel to go forth in it's purpose, and the fuel needs the system to even have purpose. </b><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Nick and Charlie </b>
</u> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736729._SX540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here's what I love about what <i>Heartstopper</i> is so far. I love that it has aspects to it that are so real in todays society, specifically pertaining to the LGBTQ+ community. It was more than just a coming of age, it was a tribute to this generation. OUR generation. <br><br>We got this movement of emotions and just as the characters were realizing things about themselves, the audience also realizes things about today. How it is okay not to be okay. <br>I never understood how things like homophobia could be a thing. And maybe that's just me.<br><br>But whenever I hear a person pissing on people who choose to love the same sex, or a different sex. <br>I always ask "Would you choose who you love because they have a different shoe size than you?" <br>*Here's when I would get the blank, confused, dumbfounded stares*<br>Then, I would say "that's just as stupid and idiotic as choosing someone to love according to their sex."<br><br>Alice Oseman, delivers that meaning through the hearts of teenage boys. She does it spectacularly. She pulls through how love is love no matter what. In a world full of hate, no one should care when a person loves another. <br>This comic touched me in every single way it possibly could, and I recommend everyone and their dog to read it. <br><br>It's safe to say, that Charlie Spring has my heart, and anyone who has the courage to come and fuck with it, can fuck with me. <br>(I have books, and I am not afraid to throw them at you. <br>yeah, I'll give you two seconds to run) <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736730._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>A Note to You</b>
</u> <br><i>Heartstopper</i> is a free read! The author posts new pages on tumblr as well as tapas! So if ever you have a spare hour, you can cruise through what's up so far. She also posts little tiny extra's and minicomics here an there and I didn't know I needed them in my life, until I saw them. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736731._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513941167i/24736732._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1514016059i/24742657._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1514016059i/24742658._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Give these two boys a chance. <br>You won't regret it.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4502148319233587612" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mX0VngSO0VF2GYfgkpwuoj3GPRjLEzJ006V8DMNHrrvPmyASNOt8UnnF8IU5ghJqWXJ8kY2/eVKzf+X7wGDR3g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1FcoGwFR3BMyB6sSoUB2Yd1O09wS7uUTjNdZch/iQNOCsR2XMTRxED3b3HcKXkqpufqSVVRCrjXsDcCFHMU/tg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12599274716332329253">Alice Oseman is an author/illustrator and was born in 1994 in Kent, England. She has written four YA contemporary novels about teenage disasters: SOLITAIRE, RADIO SILENCE, I WAS BORN FOR THIS, and LOVELESS. She is also the creator of LGBTQ+ YA romance webcomic HEARTSTOPPER, which is now published in physical form by Hachette Children's Books.<br/><br/>Alice’s first novel SOLITAIRE was published when she was</span>
  <span id="freeText12599274716332329253" style="display:none">Alice Oseman is an author/illustrator and was born in 1994 in Kent, England. She has written four YA contemporary novels about teenage disasters: SOLITAIRE, RADIO SILENCE, I WAS BORN FOR THIS, and LOVELESS. She is also the creator of LGBTQ+ YA romance webcomic HEARTSTOPPER, which is now published in physical form by Hachette Children's Books.<br /><br />Alice’s first novel SOLITAIRE was published when she was nineteen. Her YA novels have been nominated for the YA Book Prize, the Inky Awards, and the Goodreads Choice Award, and HEARTSTOPPER has been optioned for TV. She can usually be found staring aimlessly at computer screens, questioning the meaninglessness of existence, or doing anything and everything to avoid getting an office job.</span>
